            check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_naval value = 1956 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_country_flag = tbm_cat_submarines
            check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            check_variable = { var = tbm_naval_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_tech = ship_hull_rocket_submarine }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_grant_counter_extended_tech_tree_1960 value = tbm_quarterly_cap compare = less_than }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_target_year_naval value = 1956 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_tier_index value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = tbm_naval_competence value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_country_flag = tbm_cat_submarines
                has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
            }
            set_technology = { ship_hull_rocket_submarine = 1 popup = no }
            add_to_variable = { tbm_grant_counter_extended_tech_tree_1960 = 1 }
            tbm_handle_tech_grant_notification = yes
        }
    }
}
